# SEO/LLM Optimization Plan — MetalForge

**Goal:** Become the #1 resource for metal drummer gear information  
**Site:** https://metalforge.io (Vercel: metal-drummer-gear.vercel.app)

## Current Status (2026-02-07)

### ✅ Completed — Foundation (Phase 1)
- **Title & Meta:** "MetalForge - Discover What Pro Metal Drummers Play" (#19)
- **robots.txt:** Proper format with sitemap reference (#18)
- **sitemap.xml:** Dynamic generation with all drummer + gear pages (#18, #30)
- **Open Graph:** Full OG tags for social sharing
- **Twitter Card:** summary_large_image configured
- **Canonical URL:** metalforge.io set correctly
- **Google Analytics:** GA4 tracking (G-HKLHH1DCC7)

### ✅ Completed — Content Optimization (Phase 2)
- **Alt text:** All images have accessibility labels
- **Unique meta descriptions:** Dynamically generated per drummer
- **FAQ sections:** Per drummer via FAQPage schema

### ✅ Completed — Structured Data (Phase 3)
- **Person Schema:** JSON-LD for each drummer page with sameAs entity links
- **WebSite Schema:** JSON-LD for homepage
- **FAQPage Schema:** For drummer pages (#36)
- **ItemList Schema:** Collection markup for homepage (#37)
- **Product Schema:** JSON-LD for gear pages
- **BreadcrumbList Schema:** Navigation structure (#66) ✅
- **sameAs Entity Links:** Wikipedia, social profiles for LLM entity verification (#67) ✅
- **SpeakableSpecification Schema:** Voice search optimization ✅
- **VideoObject Schema:** YouTube embeds on drummer pages (#183, #186) ✅
- **Quotation Schema:** Drummer interview quotes ✅

### ✅ Completed — Performance & Media (Phase 4)
- [x] **Core Web Vitals optimization** — #442 ✅
  - YouTube facade pattern (500KB+ savings per embed)
  - Above-fold image preloading
  - Enhanced CLS prevention for videos/images
  - INP optimizations for faster interactions
  - YouTube preconnect hints
- [x] **Image optimization** (WebP, lazy loading) — #323 ✅

### ✅ Completed — Entity Relationships (Phase 5a)
- [x] **MusicGroup schema** linking drummers to bands — #517 ✅

### 📋 Future Enhancements (Phase 5b — Feature-Dependent)
- [ ] AggregateRating for gear items (requires user reviews feature)
- [ ] HowTo schema for gear setup guides (if content added)
- [ ] SearchAction schema for site search (if implemented)

---

| Phase | Focus | Status |

## Metrics to Track
- Google Search Console impressions/clicks
- Rich result appearances
- AI citation frequency (manual tracking)
- Core Web Vitals scores (LCP, FID, CLS)
- Lighthouse Performance score

## Notes
- Ralph (AI agent) auto-fixes issues with `ai-fix` label
- SEO agent runs daily at 8AM (Lisboa timezone)
- All structured data uses schema.org vocabulary
- 21 drummers currently with bios, gear, videos, endorsements

- **2026-06-18 (run 6):** 🔍 **SEO Agent run (Week 4) — FULL AGGRESSIVE MODE: 10 net-new proposals filed.** GSC active (1,115 impr / 1.70% CTR / pos 8.4). CEO triaged 20 proposals in today's 07:10 + 13:00 pulses; 10 untriaged from the 02:00 run still pending CEO review (#1324-#1333). ai-fix queue at 17 active. Deep code audit this run uncovered two previously unknown systemic gaps.
  - **Audit:** robots.txt (`api/robots.js`) — all **8 AI crawlers** present ✅. LLM surface: `index.md`+`faq.md`+`gear-guide.md`+`licks.md`+`techniques.md`+`bands.md`+`gear-by-brand.md`+`comparisons.md`+`facts.md`+`lists.md`+`quiz.md`+`gear-series/`+`tools/`(5 files)+`articles/`+`licks/`(53 files)+`drummers/`(61 files). `/llms/vs/` is empty — #1276 approved but not yet shipped. `/llms/tools/name-generator.md` absent (all 5 other tool .md files present). 78 extendedBios.js entries with `metaTitle` overrides — ALL say "Biography". Quick Facts live. Sitemap comprehensive.
  - **🔴 Critical finding — extendedBios.js metaTitle override bug (#1346):** Verified `App.js:11855` sets `document.title = bio.metaTitle` client-side, overriding the SSR keyword-matched title. ALL ~78 extendedBios.js `metaTitle` values say "Biography - [Band] Drummer". When Googlebot executes JavaScript, it sees "Ben Koller Biography" instead of "Ben Koller Drum Kit & Gear Setup". **GSC proof:** "ben koller drum setup" pos 3.3 at 0% CTR — page is on page 1 but title mismatch kills CTR. Same issue for Inferno ("behemoth drum kit" pos 9.0, 0% CTR) and all ~78 extended-bio drummers. The #1158 template fix helped non-override drummers but all override drummers still have "Biography" titles.
  - **🟠 Critical finding — lick pages SSR schema invisible (#1347):** All 157 lick pages have rich `@graph` JSON-LD (HowTo + VideoObject + MusicRecording + BreadcrumbList) via `generateLickSchema()` in App.js. But App.js is client-side-only — `api/meta/[...path].js` lick handler (line 589) returns no `articleSchema` → zero JSON-LD in SSR. Same bug class as #1189 (vs comparison pages, SHIPPED). Crawlers see no schema on 157 lick pages.
  - **Hub SSR meta gaps verified:** `/vs` hub (sitemap priority 0.9) and `/guides` hub (sitemap priority 0.9) both have no `path === '/vs'` or `path === '/guides'` handlers — fall to generic SPA fallback. Filed #1348/#1349.
  - **Tool sub-pages SSR meta gaps verified:** `/tools/gear-search`, `/tools/dream-set-builder`, `/tools/tier-list`, `/tools/name-generator` — all sitemapped at priority 0.95 but no SSR meta handlers (only `/tools/signature-licks` and `/tools/kit-builder` have handlers). Filed #1350.
  - **GSC signal:** 1,115 impr / 19 clicks / 1.70% CTR / pos 8.4 (slight dip from 1.94% — expected indexing lag). Primary gap: "joey jordison drum set" 118 impr @ 0.85% CTR pos 9.0. Secondary: "ben koller drum setup" pos 3.3 / 0% CTR — **title mismatch confirmed, root cause identified**.
  - **Filed #1346** (🔴 batch, ~78 drummers): extendedBios.js metaTitle overrides — all "Biography" titles override SSR. Ben Koller pos 3.3/0% CTR + Inferno pos 9.0/0% CTR are GSC signals exposing a roster-wide issue.
  - **Filed #1347** (🟠 batch, ~157 pages): lick pages SSR schema — HowTo + VideoObject + MusicRecording JSON-LD is client-side only, crawlers see zero schema. Add `articleSchema` to SSR handler.
  - **Filed #1348** (🟠 atomic): `/vs` hub SSR meta + CollectionPage schema — sitemap priority 0.9, no handler.

  - **GSC readout (first-ever real query data):** 1,279 impr / 32 clicks / 2.50% CTR / pos 8.6. Dominant intent is unmistakable: **"`<drummer>` drum kit / drum set / setup / gear."** Joey Jordison alone ≈129 impr (~10% of all impressions), all stuck **pos 6–9**. CEO already filed **#1140** (Joey-specific editorial title/meta/content/links).
  - **🔴 STRUCTURAL FINDING (the headline) — filed #1141:** audited the **actual served HTML** (not just code) and found **every drummer page serves an identical generic SPA shell to crawlers.** `curl -A Googlebot https://metalforge.io/drummer/joey-jordison` → `<title>MetalForge - Discover What Pro Metal Drummers Play</title>` + the homepage's stale "50+ pro drummers" meta description + **6.5KB shell, "Joey Jordison" appears once, zero per-page og/JSON-LD/content.** Per-drummer title ("Joey Jordison Drum Kit & Gear Setup", `ogMetaTags.js:145`) + content only exist **after client-side JS**. Root cause (2 layers): (1) `vercel.json:293` rewrites every content path → `/index.html`; no bot/UA rewrite. (2) The prerender handler `api/meta/[...path].js` exists with correct per-page logic but **returns generic even when hit directly** (`/api/meta/drummer/joey-jordison` → generic title) — `getDrummerBySlug` resolves null in the deployed fn, so it needs **fixing**, not just wiring.
  - **Why #1141 is the highest-leverage item now:** **no-JS AI crawlers (GPTBot/ClaudeBot/PerplexityBot — this agent's core mission) see only the generic shell — every drummer page is byte-identical to them.** `/llms/*.md` partly mitigates, but the canonical drummer URLs are invisible/indistinguishable to AI crawlers. For Google (renders JS, so Joey ranks) it's a reliability/first-pass-title win on exactly the GSC-validated pos-5–9 cluster. Proposed phased fix: fix the handler's data resolution, then a **crawler-only** `has: user-agent` rewrite routing `/drummer/:slug` → `/api/meta/...` (handler already redirects humans → bots-safe). Included dynamic-rendering/cloaking caveat + 5 verify checks. Complements #1140 (which currently only lands via JS render) by fixing the crawler-visible layer for the **whole roster**.

  - **Audit — first live Lighthouse run:** `npx lighthouse` (SEO category only) against production on homepage + `/drummer/joey-jordison` + `/articles/most-expensive-drum-setups` → **92/100 on all three**, identical failing audit each time: **`robots-txt` scores 0 ("robots.txt is not valid")**. Root cause (`api/robots.js`): the `Content-Signal: ai-train=yes, search=yes, ai-input=yes` line (appears twice — once site-wide at line 1, once repeated inside the `User-agent: *` block) and `Video-Sitemap: https://metalforge.io/video-sitemap.xml` are both flagged "Unknown directive" by Lighthouse's robots.txt parser. `Content-Signal` is a legitimate emerging spec (draft-romm-aipref-contentsignals) but isn't recognized by standard robots.txt validators (Google's included) as an in-file directive — worth revisiting as an HTTP response header instead of (or in addition to) an in-body directive, and dropping the duplicate line + the non-standard `Video-Sitemap:` line. **Not filed this run** (bank ≥40) — flagging here so the next sub-40 run files it as a 🔴-adjacent single fix (`api/robots.js`, ~10 line change, no template/data work).

- **2026-07-05:** 🔍 **SEO Agent run — BANK REFILL MODE: 3 net-new proposals filed (#3711/#3712/#3713), including a 🔴 CRITICAL re-diagnosis of a stale-closed issue.** Open `seo-proposal` bank was **6** at run start (well under the 45 cap) — refilled to 9.
  - **🔴 Filed #3711 — the headline finding this run.** Live curl audit (not just a code/grep audit) of production against 4 real bot User-Agents (`Googlebot`, `GPTBot`, `ClaudeBot`, `PerplexityBot`) across 5 page types (`/drummer/joey-jordison`, `/articles/fastest-double-bass-drummers`, `/battles`, `/drummers`, `/gear/tama`, plus `/` itself) found **every single one serves the identical 6,849-byte generic SPA shell** — same title, same etag, **zero JSON-LD** anywhere, including the homepage (which per this very plan's Phase-3 section should have `WebSite` schema). This is the exact bug `#1141` (filed 2026-06-16, GSC-grounded, approved as highest-leverage) claimed to fix — but `#1141` was closed the same instant as an unrelated bulk-scope PR (#1170), and `git log --all --grep="1141"` shows **no implementing commit ever landed**. Root cause newly diagnosed: `vercel.json`'s catch-all rewrite (`/:path* → /index.html`, no `/api/` exclusion) swallows even direct hits to `/api/meta/drummer/joey-jordison` (same cached file, same etag as the homepage) — so the fully-built-out `api/meta/[...path].js` handler (drummers/articles/bands/techniques/licks/lists/gear/guides/evolution/battles/quotes/genre-gear-guides, 1000+ lines) has literally never been reachable. This is the **third stale-closure catch** this week (after Axenrot SoundLike and comparison-pairs #2198) but by far the highest-severity — it's the structural ceiling on the entire LLM-citation mission, since GPTBot/ClaudeBot/PerplexityBot/anthropic-ai (all explicitly welcomed in `robots.txt`) get zero facts from any dynamic HTML page today; `/llms/*.md` is carrying the entire non-JS-crawler-facing load by itself. Scoped the fix narrowly (matching #1141's own original Phase-1 scope): (1) exclude `/api/` from the vercel.json catch-all, (2) add one crawler-only `has`-header rewrite for `/drummer/:slug` → `/api/meta/drummer/:slug`. 5 verify checks included, explicit no-cloaking check (browser UA must stay unaffected).
  - **Filed #3712** (🟠 batch, 3 profiles + 3 LLM files): Drummer Evolution batch 24 — Chris Turner, Isaac Lamb, Jocke Wallgren. On the profile page itself it silently falls back to a hardcoded 3-slug list (`lars-ulrich`, `joey-jordison`, `dave-lombardo`) even though `GEAR_PRICE_HISTORY` has 67 drummers' worth of data — so ~64 drummer profile pages have never linked to their own gear-history sub-page. ## 2026-07-09 20:30 — Bank at 9 (all real proposals already carry `ai-fix`), filed 1 CRITICAL live-verified bug: Evans/Remo brand pages serving generic shell

- **Bank check:** 9 open `seo-proposal` at run start — checked labels, not just the count: 2211/3810/3819 are trackers, and all 6 real proposals (#4160/#4161/#4162/#4169/#4180/#4182) already carry `ai-fix` (promoted, awaiting/in PR) — true untriaged bank is effectively 0. Well under the 45 cap → filed up to 8; chose 1 high-confidence, thoroughly-verified item over forcing volume, consistent with the "quality over volume" guidance and several prior runs' precedent.
- **Live audit:** `robots.txt` (`api/robots.js`) — all 8 AI crawlers + Claude-Web explicitly allowed, no regression. `/llms/`: 62/62 drummer profiles + 25 root-level category/index files. Chased down a false alarm: bot-UA curls on `/genre/black-metal`, `/genre/death-metal`, `/genre/thrash-metal` etc. returned the generic homepage shell — looked like a fresh crawler-shell regression, but root-caused it as **my own bad test input**, not a bug: `genres.js`'s real slugs are short-form (`thrash`, `death`, `black`, `progressive`, `nu-metal`, `groove`, `metalcore`, `hardcore`, `technical-death`), not the `-metal`-suffixed slugs used by the unrelated `genreGearGuides.js` vocabulary. Re-tested with the correct 9 slugs — all render correct per-page titles + 2 JSON-LD blocks each. No regression; other route families (`/vs`, `/guides`, `/technique`, `/battles`, `/bands`, `/lists`) also confirmed correct on spot-check. Logging this so a future run doesn't repeat the same wrong-slug false positive.
- **Genuine finding (live-verified, not agent-reported):** `curl -A "GPTBot/1.0" https://metalforge.io/brands/evans` and `/brands/remo` both return **200 with the generic homepage title and zero JSON-LD** — indexable-but-thin, the worst SEO state. Root-caused across 3 files: `BRAND_META` in `api/meta/[...path].js` (~line 1697), `gearBrands` in `api/sitemap.js` (~line 155), and `BRAND_SEO_DATA` in `packages/frontend/data/gearSearchData.js` (~line 226) all hardcode the same 8 brands (tama/pearl/dw/ludwig/zildjian/paiste/meinl/sabian) — Evans and Remo were never added to any of the three, so human visitors also see "Brand not found" (`GearSearchmd.js:1050` gates on `BRAND_SEO_DATA`), not just bots. Verified this is NOT thin content once fixed: `GEAR_INDEX_BRAND_LEVEL` (already built and live via #3714) has real, verified data — **31 drummers use Evans, 18 use Remo** (`node -e "import('./packages/frontend/data/gearIndex.js').then(m=>console.log(m.GEAR_INDEX_BRAND_LEVEL.Evans.length, m.GEAR_INDEX_BRAND_LEVEL.Remo.length))"` → 31 18), clearing the bar with far more margin than some of the existing 8 brands. Confirmed not a duplicate of closed #3714 (which shipped the *different* `/gear/evans/all-drumheads/drummers-using` route, never touched `/brands/<slug>`) or #1408/#1383 (built the original 8-brand pipeline before Evans/Remo had any drumhead data).
- **Scope discipline:** deliberately did NOT propose wiring Evans/Remo into `GEAR_DATABASE`/`DRUMMER_GEAR` (the separate hand-authored commercial product catalog behind the Gear Search/Compare tool, #719/#721) — that would mean inventing drumhead SKUs/prices with no real source. ## 2026-07-10 (bank-capped run) — root roster-drift audit: found 5 concrete, evidence-backed gaps

### Context
Bank check: 6 open `seo-proposal` issues, but only 3 are real actionable proposals (#4180 endorsement tracker, #4161 comparison pairs, #4160 Casagrande album-arc — all still open/unshipped); the other 3 are standing umbrella trackers (#3819, #3810, #2211). Well under the 45 floor → filed up to 8, chose 5 high-confidence proposals over padding to the cap.

Priority-framework issues #870–#874 (technique pages, gear-brand pages, Quick Facts, `/llms/<drummer>.md`, internal-linking blocks) are all **CLOSED/shipped**. Metrics show no GSC content-gap rows this week (impr≥50, CTR<2%) — clean, so this run focused on a root-cause data-integrity audit instead of a specific query gap.

### What I found (all independently verified via Node eval / grep diff, not assumed)
Followed up on the prior run's note about `stats.md`/`index.md` staleness and found the actual root cause runs deeper than date drift:
- **`api/sitemap.js`'s hardcoded drummer roster array (lines 67–89) has only 61 entries vs. 65 in `api/drummers/index.js`** — diffed both arrays by name. Missing: Martin Axenrot, Paul Bostaph, Sean Reinert, Nick Menza. All 4 have full profile data (bio/gear/kitOverview) and are cited elsewhere (licks, guides, FAQ, birthdays.md) but have **zero XML sitemap entry** — a real indexation gap, not just a content gap.
- **`public/llms/drummers/` has 62/65 files** — same 3 missing (Bostaph/Reinert/Menza; Axenrot's file already exists). Root cause: `scripts/generate-llms-drummers.cjs` reads dynamically from `api/drummers/index.js` (no hardcoded roster) — it's already correct, just hasn't been re-run since these 3 were added to the API.
- **Content-accuracy bug in `public/llms/bpm.md`**: 4 rows for Rust in Peace / Countdown to Extinction tracks display "Nick Menza" but link to `/drummer/dirk-verbeuren` (Megadeth's much-later drummer). Source data `metalSongsBpm.js` is correct (`drummer: "nick-menza"`) — bug is isolated to the generated markdown. Same class as #4191 (Daray/Dimmu Borgir), which the CEO promoted same-day.
- **3rd occurrence of the stale-hub-file bug**: `index.md` (2026-06-19, "63 drummers"/"15 tracked" claims), `stats.md` (2026-06-18, "61 drummers"), and `llms.txt` ("63 drummers"/"61 comparisons"/"15 metal drummers") are all stale vs. live data — same bug class as #4192 (endorsements.md hub), now caught a 2nd and 3rd time.
- **Systemic root cause**: 23 generator scripts in `scripts/generate-llms-*.cjs` produce the entire `/llms/` surface, but none are wired into `package.json` or any `.github/workflows/*.yml` — confirmed via grep, zero hits. Nothing catches drift automatically; it's only ever found by manual audit (3 times now in 2 runs).

### Filed this run
1. #4201 — SEO: Add 4 missing drummers to XML sitemap roster (Axenrot, Bostaph, Reinert, Menza)
2. #4202 — SEO: Generate 3 missing /llms/drummers/*.md files (Bostaph, Reinert, Menza)
3. #4203 — SEO: Fix 4 broken Nick Menza links in /llms/bpm.md (point to Dirk Verbeuren instead)
4. #4204 — SEO: Regenerate stale /llms/index.md, /llms/stats.md, /llms.txt drummer/roster counts
5. #4205 — SEO: Add CI check to catch /llms/*.md hub files going stale (root-cause fix)

### Next run
- #4201/#4202 should land together or #4201 first — sitemap discoverability is the higher-value half.
- #4205 (CI drift-check) is the highest-leverage fix of the 5 — if it ships, this exact audit vein (stale hub files, roster drift) retires as a recurring proposal source. Don't re-run this same audit until #4205 ships or a meaningful amount of new drummer/data content is added.
- Once #4201/#4202 ship, Nick Menza/Paul Bostaph/Sean Reinert become fully onboarded (65/65 sitemap + llms coverage) — worth a fresh comparison-pairs/endorsement-tracker gap check against the *new* 65-drummer roster (not just the 62 used by #4161/#4180), but only after those ship to avoid duplicate proposals.
- Bank goes from 3 real actionable proposals to 8 this run (5 new + #4180/#4161/#4160 still pending CEO triage).

### What I found (all independently verified via node eval / grep diff, not assumed)
- **`public/llms/licks.md` hub generator (`scripts/generate-llms-licks.cjs`) is silently broken** — its regex expects a literal `export const SIGNATURE_LICKS = {...}` in `signatureLicks.js`, but that file was refactored under #1056 to `import { SIGNATURE_LICKS } from './licks/index.js'; export { SIGNATURE_LICKS };` — no literal exists anymore. Running the script today would hit the null-check and `process.exit(1)`. Confirmed via the file's own stale header (`Last updated: 2026-06-13`, last git-touched by #3700) and confirmed 0 mentions of Adrian Erlandsson/Sean Reinert (both live since #4114/#2219) in the current `licks.md`.

- **`generate-llms-endorsements.cjs`'s `TARGET_SLUGS` hardcoded list has drifted to 38 vs 65 live `ENDORSEMENT_TIMELINE` entries** — confirmed via node-eval of the array plus a grep diff against `endorsementNews.js`. - **Finding 1 (#4371) + Finding 2 (#4372):** Delegated a systematic sweep of every static route in `App.js` against vercel.json rewrites / `api/meta/[...path].js` branches / `api/sitemap.js` entries (same bug class as #4368/#4370). Root cause: `generateArticleSchema()` in `api/meta/[...path].js:3910` has two modes — string (verbatim `@graph`, used by the `isArticle`-flagged top10/`​/lists/:slug` branches) vs. object (auto-builds full `Article` schema + `article:published_time` OG tags, used by `ARTICLE_METADATA`/`ALBUM_ARTICLES`/`/vs/:slug`). The string-mode branches never surface the `datePublished`/`dateModified` fields that already exist in `top10Lists.js` (verified present, e.g. lines 111-112) — pure wiring gap, no missing content. Affects 12 `/articles/:slug` (isArticle) + 98 `/lists/:slug` = 110 sitemap-priority-0.9 pages missing dated/attributed Article schema that every structurally similar page on the site already has.
- **False positives caught before filing (good — verification worked as intended):** raw `grep -c "date:"` on `gearNews.js` showed 22 vs hub's "21 total events" — looked like recurrence of the already-closed #4293, but the 22nd match was a non-data mapping-function line (`date: item.date,`); actual data count is 21, matches. `gear-history.md`'s 68 `## ` headers vs 67 drummers — one heading is a section title, not a drummer entry, matches. `guides.md`'s 74 sections vs 115 files in `public/llms/guides/` — the 115 includes an unrelated "best-X-for-metal" gear-guide content type never meant to be in `guides.md`, not a gap. All three would have been wasted/incorrect proposals had they been filed on raw counts alone.
